### Comment by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) — 2023-05-17T17:57:56Z

I would suggest that priority/preemption always go first. Otherwise we have a priority inversion, if a lower priority job prevents higher priority job from using the full potential of the cluster.  If we want to give the users an option to be nice and use lower concurrency to avoid preemptions, it should be a separate setting. 

Ideally, in the fullness of time, we should have 3 settings for a job:

- (`A`) Bare Minimum number of pods
- (`B`) Decent number of pods 
- (`C`) Desired number of pods

A job would start only if it can get `A` pods, would preempt other jobs only until the parallelism reaches  `B`. The job would ideally try to go up to `C` but would not preempt anyone once above `B`. 

For now, I think we can assume that `B==C`. `A==C` would be a bit less intuitive, IMHO.

### Comment by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-25T17:59:17Z

The only outstanding question is whether we want to allow more than one PodSet to have partial admission.

JobSet and RayJob might benefit from such behavior, although it's unclear what should be the desired policy to avoid an exhaustive search.

Let's proceed with this for now and we can revisit during implementation.

/lgtm
/approve

## Reviews

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-11T15:30:58Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:110** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-11T15:30:58Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`
```

  is this a number or just a boolean? If a number, a better name would be `/min-count`?
  Check https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/scheduler-plugins/blob/master/kep/42-podgroup-coscheduling/README.md and https://volcano.sh/en/docs/podgroup/ for inspiration

+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  What happens with the job when admitted? do we update parallelism and completions?
  Also, completions is immutable unless parallelism is set at the same time.
  
  https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/workloads/controllers/job/#elastic-indexed-jobs
  
  Also only possible for Indexed Jobs. So we need to validate that in the webhook.
  
  Any notes for MPIJob?

```

  > What happens with the job when admitted?
  
  The way I see it, since the batch user opts in  for partial admission , he/she is aware that the `parallelism` can change at runtime and populate  `completions` with the actual number of successful runs needed.  Or our job  default webhook can copy parallelism to completions  when the annotation is set.
  
  > Also only possible for Indexed Jobs. So we need to validate that in the webhook.
  
  I think it should work for non indexed jobs as well.
  
  > Any notes for MPIJob?
  
  No, I think is better to target the core part of Kueue and batch/Job as a reference implementation.

++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`
```

  I see it more as a `bool`, when true the `MinimumCount` of the podset will be set to 1.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-12T13:35:47Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:110** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-12T13:35:46Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`
```

  I don't think that's flexible enough. Some users might want to set a minimum higher than 1.
  For example: "I want to run with 10 pods, but I'm ok with at least 5"

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-12T13:39:22Z

+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)

+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->

+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  > The way I see it, since the batch user opts in for partial admission , he/she is aware that the `parallelism` can change at runtime and populate `completions` with the actual number of successful runs needed.
  
  That reminds me that there are actually two scenarios:
  - highly parallel jobs, where every index can run on its own. Then just modifying parallelism is good enough.
  - jobs with pod-to-pod communication. Here all pods need to start together, then both parallelism and completions need to change.

+### batch/Job controller
```

  > No, I think is better to target the core part of Kueue and batch/Job as a reference implementation.
  
  In a design doc, it's sometimes useful to see the bigger picture. We don't want to get stuck with an API that only works for one use case.
  
  Implementation PRs can certainly be separate for Job and MPIJob.

### Review by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) (commented) — 2023-05-15T08:21:39Z

+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
```

  done

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:131** by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) — 2023-05-15T06:00:45Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  > * jobs with pod-to-pod communication. Here all pods need to start together, then both parallelism and completions need to change.
  
  I can't say I fully understand this, however what we could do tho improve the overall situation is to add an extra check in kueue'd job web-hook and fail the validation when partial admission is accepted but  `completions` is not explicitly provided.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:110** by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) — 2023-05-15T07:12:11Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`
```

  updated

```

  In regards to preemption the following approaches could be taken into account.
  
  1. The full workload is admissible with preemption:
     1.A. **try partial  admission**
            1.A.a. **partial admission is possible without preemption, accept partial admission**
             1.A.b. partial admission is not possible  without preemption
             1.A.b.1 **accept the full preemption solution**
             1.A.b.1 accept a partial with preemption solution
     1.B  full preemption solution
  
  The **bold** items are implemented in my WIP implementation.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:118** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2023-05-16T05:43:01Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)

+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
+- rework the webhook to validate that `completions` is provided in case partial admission is accepted.
+
+### kubeflow/MPIJob controller
+
+In case of MPIJob `j.Spec.RunPolicy.SchedulingPolicy.MinAvailable` can be used to provide a `minimumCount` for the `Worker` podsSet while updating `j.Spec.MPIReplicaSpecs[kubeflow.MPIReplicaTypeWorker].Replicas` before unsuspending  the job and after suspending it.
```

  ```suggestion
  In case of MPIJob `j.Spec.RunPolicy.SchedulingPolicy.MinAvailable` can be used to provide a `minimumCount` for the `Worker` podsSet while updating `j.Spec.MPIReplicaSpecs[kubeflow.MPIReplicaTypeWorker].Replicas` before unsuspending the job and after suspending it.
  ```

+

++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}

+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.

+

```

  ```suggestion
  Whether an MPIJob supports partial admission or not can be deduced based on `MinAvailable` without the need of a dedicated annotation.
  ```
  
  The `SchedulingPolicy` in the MPIJob isn't designed only for gang scheduling. So we should mention `MinAvailable`.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:57** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-16T20:08:47Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.

+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.

+### Goals

+
+### Non-Goals
+

+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.

+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
```

  I think we should try to minimize preemption.
  
  But there are two forms of preemption: within ClusterQueue and within cohort.
  
  ### within Cluster Queue
  
  I agree with the chosen option for 1.A.a
  But we should do 1.A.b.2: accept a partial admission with preemption
  
  ### within cohort
  
  In this case, the ClusterQueue could be reclaiming quota that belongs to it by doing preemption before going into partial admission.
  
  Can we do this distinction? The implementation might be a bit more complex.
  
  cc @ahg-g and @mwielgus for comment on the correct semantics.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:72** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-16T20:09:24Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
```

  Let's also validate that only one podset can have this parameter set.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:84** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-16T20:10:25Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
```

  We should do binary search to find the maximum number of parallelism that is feasible.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:112** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-16T20:14:52Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
```

  can you provide an example of this? Are you saying that the `accept-partial-admission` should contain a number?

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:120** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-16T20:16:12Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
+- rework the webhook to validate that `completions` is provided in case partial admission is accepted.
+
+### kubeflow/MPIJob controller
+
+In case of MPIJob `j.Spec.RunPolicy.SchedulingPolicy.MinAvailable` can be used to provide a `minimumCount` for the `Worker` podsSet while updating `j.Spec.MPIReplicaSpecs[kubeflow.MPIReplicaTypeWorker].Replicas` before unsuspending  the job and after suspending it.
+
+Whether an MPIJob supports partial admission  or not can be deduced based on  `SchedulingPolicy` without the need of a dedicated annotation.
```

  If we can use `minAvailable`, that would be better.

+
+```go

+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1

+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
```

  done,
  
  the implementation uses binary search.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:112** by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) — 2023-05-17T08:10:00Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
```

  changed to `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism` , should make more sense.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:118** by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) — 2023-05-17T08:10:09Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
+- rework the webhook to validate that `completions` is provided in case partial admission is accepted.
+
+### kubeflow/MPIJob controller
+
+In case of MPIJob `j.Spec.RunPolicy.SchedulingPolicy.MinAvailable` can be used to provide a `minimumCount` for the `Worker` podsSet while updating `j.Spec.MPIReplicaSpecs[kubeflow.MPIReplicaTypeWorker].Replicas` before unsuspending  the job and after suspending it.
```

  done

+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
+- rework the webhook to validate that `completions` is provided in case partial admission is accepted.
+
+### kubeflow/MPIJob controller
+
+In case of MPIJob `j.Spec.RunPolicy.SchedulingPolicy.MinAvailable` can be used to provide a `minimumCount` for the `Worker` podsSet while updating `j.Spec.MPIReplicaSpecs[kubeflow.MPIReplicaTypeWorker].Replicas` before unsuspending  the job and after suspending it.
+
+Whether an MPIJob supports partial admission  or not can be deduced based on  `SchedulingPolicy` without the need of a dedicated annotation.
```

  > The SchedulingPolicy in the MPIJob isn't designed only for gang scheduling. So we should mention MinAvailable.
  
  done
  
  >If we can use minAvailable, that would be better.

+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
```

  I was discussing this offline with @mwielgus and he convinced me that preemption should have higher priority.
  
  In the case of cohort, the ClusterQueue is reclaiming quota that belongs to it, so it certainly should preempt.
  In the case of higher priority within the ClusterQueue, the Workload has higher priority, so it should preempt. Otherwise it would depend on the order in which workloads come in:
  - if low priority comes first, it's running and the higher priority workload has less pods.
  - if high priority comes first, then it has a big number of pods and low priority doesn't run.
  
  Prioritizing preemption has the effect of behaving similar to the case where the high priority workload comes first.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-17T17:21:04Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:72** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-17T17:21:03Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,148 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
```

  I know, but I don't think the current proposed implementation scales well.
  We need to do binary search.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-17T17:24:12Z

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)

+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)

+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
