+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  > 
  
  Oh I missed this.
  
  Jobs with pod-to-pod communication are jobs where all pods within the job communicate with each other. In this case, it doesn't make sense to have `parallelism!=completions`.
  
  So this gives us two different use cases of partial admission:
  - I accept lower level of parallelism, but keep number of completions.
  - I accept lower level of parallelism and it should remain equal to number of completions.

+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals

+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. +
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not fit in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the count did not reach the `MinimumCount`, try to find a combination of counts that fits. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
```

  Can you provide a high level summary of how you plan to implement "try a combination of counts that fits"?
  
  I know you have a working PR, but it might be helpful to lay down some high level idea here, both to being able to spot design flaws and to have a future reference.
  
  Here is an example of the level of detail that I'm looking for https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/tree/main/keps/83-workload-preemption#changes-in-scheduling-algorithm
  It might be simpler for this problem.

+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)

+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)

+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/accept-partial-admission`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` and other aspect that should be taken into consideration like elastic index jobs.
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
+- rework the webhook to validate that `completions` is provided in case partial admission is accepted.
+
+### kubeflow/MPIJob controller
+
+In case of MPIJob `j.Spec.RunPolicy.SchedulingPolicy.MinAvailable` can be used to provide a `minimumCount` for the `Worker` podsSet while updating `j.Spec.MPIReplicaSpecs[kubeflow.MPIReplicaTypeWorker].Replicas` before unsuspending  the job and after suspending it.
+
+Whether an MPIJob supports partial admission  or not can be deduced based on  `SchedulingPolicy` without the need of a dedicated annotation.
```

  > If we can use minAvailable, that would be better.
  
  Agree. If we can do that, we should select the way.

```

  In this case , we should not enforce anything on the  `completion` field in the webhook, and the user should ensure that `parallelism` == `completions` for the first case leave the `completions` nil for the second.

+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
```

  we have bynary search with support for multiple variable count  podsets.

+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not fit in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the count did not reach the `MinimumCount`, try to find a combination of counts that fits. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
```

+type PodSet struct {

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:106** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-18T19:50:30Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,162 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
```

  Are you saying that both podsets would be resized proportionally?
  
  What if podset B requires a set of resources that are not under usage, whereas podset C requires resizing?
  
  would it be possible to have podset B with 100%, but podset C with 50%?

```

  One design detail that is missing here is whether you are doing the search within one scheduling cycle or across multiple scheduling cycles?
  
  I ask this because, before this feature, we don't know if preemption would help until we finish the scheduling cycle. Are you changing this behavior in a drastic way?

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@

+

+<!-- /toc -->

+## Summary

+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation

+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals

+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  nil `completions` has a specific meaning in the Job API https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/workloads/controllers/job/#parallel-jobs
  
  The second use case I might or might not have `completions` set. If it's not set, you are right, we can just change parallelism. But if completions is set, users might want completions to also change.
  
  I think the solution is to have another annotation that indicates whether completions should be changed too, and validate that `parallelism == completions` when this annotation is set.

### Review by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) (commented) — 2023-05-19T06:09:12Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:79** by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) — 2023-05-19T05:41:49Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,162 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
```

  done

+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.

+
+### Goals

+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional

+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
```

  All is happening in one scheduling cycle (it should now be reflected in the content), The preemption is not changed in any way.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:106** by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) — 2023-05-19T05:52:32Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,162 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
```

  It wold be possible, but the search will become a lot more complex.

+    // for this PodSet

+}
+

+

The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`

+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  I meant the one that needs to keep `parallelism` and `completions` in sync.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-19T14:32:36Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:131** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-19T14:32:36Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,139 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add and optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then jobs should still be admitted.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+TBD: It should be decided if the partial admission should be taken into account before attempting preemption. Since preemption has its own penalties (time to evict the active workloads, potential waste of the resources used by the preempted workloads) I vote to take it into account before.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount the minimum caount acceoted for this
+    // PodSet in case of partial admission.
+    // If not provided, partial admission is not accepted
+    // for this PodSet
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+I case the current workload dose not in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission and the cont did not reach the `MinimumCount`, decrease the cont in one PodSet and try again. The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are published in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
```

  There is nothing that keeps them in sync. It's just one way that users can use the fields.
  
  But somewhat related are these:
  - https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/workloads/controllers/job/#elastic-indexed-jobs
  - https://kubernetes.io/docs/tasks/job/job-with-pod-to-pod-communication/

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-19T18:58:47Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:106** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-19T18:58:47Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,162 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
```

  Right, but then I'm not sure the behavior would be clear to users.
  I would prefer we limit scaling to one podset, until we have a known use case for more than one.

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the workload proposed for the current scheduling cycle, does not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
+
+
+The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are recorded in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` acceptable by the job in case of partial admission.
+  * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/sync-completions`
```

  ```suggestion
    * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-completions-equal-parallelism`
  ```
  
  @ahg-g wdyt?

+```go

+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1

+

+    // in case of partial admission.

+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.

+Starting with the PodSets:

+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}

+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
```

  This looks weird to me. I think we have 3 options like the below:
  
  - As @alculquicondor says, limit scaling to one podSet.
  - Admit podSets based on each priorityClass if priorityClass is set in each podSet.
  - Admit podSets based on the order determined by the Workload resource similar to behavior when assigning flavor.

### Review by [@trasc](https://github.com/trasc) (commented) — 2023-05-22T09:43:27Z

+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
```

  > Admit podSets based on each priorityClass if priorityClass is set in each podSet.
  
  Currently we are using priority class per workload...., 
  
  > Admit podSets based on the order determined by the Workload resource similar to behavior when assigning flavor.
  
  We cannot compare this to flavor assignment,  if the flavor assignment fails on the last podSet the entire workload will be requeued.

### Review by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) (commented) — 2023-05-22T11:59:07Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:106** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2023-05-22T11:59:07Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,162 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
```

  > Currently we are using priority class per workload....,
  
  Uhm.. that's right...
  
  > We cannot compare this to flavor assignment, if the flavor assignment fails on the last podSet the entire workload will be requeued.
  
  Can we ignore assignment errors only when partial admission?

+### Workload API

+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the current workload dose not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.

+Starting with the PodSets:

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:128** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2023-05-23T06:26:55Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories](#user-stories)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the workload proposed for the current scheduling cycle, does not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
+
+
+The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are recorded in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` acceptable by the job in case of partial admission.
+  * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/sync-completions`
```

  Perhaps the integration controller defaults `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-completions-equal-parallelism` to true if the job was created with `parallelism=completions`.

+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.

++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...

+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` acceptable by the job in case of partial admission.
+  * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/sync-completions`
```

  I'm not sure we can imply this. You could have an embarrassingly parallel job where you ideally want maximum parallelism, but are ok with less.
  I think it's better for the user to be explicit about the semantics they want, given that parallelism and completions are separate fields to begin with

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:138** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-23T14:22:01Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)

+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Workload API](#workload-api)
+  - [Scheduler / Flavorassignment](#scheduler--flavorassignment)
+  - [Jobframework](#jobframework)
+  - [batch/Job controller](#batchjob-controller)
+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the workload proposed for the current scheduling cycle, does not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
+
+
+The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are recorded in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` acceptable by the job in case of partial admission.
+  * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/sync-completions`
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
```

  Evaluate whether we can remove this function from the framework, by just using `GetPodSets`.
  
  Work on it on a separate implementation PR.

+    // enabled.

+}
+

+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the workload proposed for the current scheduling cycle, does not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.

+

++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.

++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+

+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` acceptable by the job in case of partial admission.
+  * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/sync-completions`
```

  This is just defaulting, they can set `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-completions-equal-parallelism=false` if they don't wish to; so the question is more about who we think will use parallelism=completions more often.

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:140** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2023-05-23T15:19:03Z

@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)

+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
+### Goals
+
+Provide an opt-in way for Workloads to accept the admission with a lower count of pods if the full count is not available.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Since this is an opt-in feature, the parent job should accept the partial admission parameters provided by Kueue.
+
+Kueue will not take any measure to ensure that the parent job respects the assigned quota.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Change the way the flavor assigner work to support decrementing the pods count in order to find a better fit for the current workload.
+In case a partial fit is chosen, the jobframework reconciler should provide the admitted pod counts to the parent job before unsuspending it, in a similar fashion as the node selectors are provided. In case the job gets suspended, the original pod counts should be restored in order to allow a potential future admission with its original pod counts.
+
+### User Stories
+
+Kueue issue [420](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/420) provides details on the initial feature details and its applicability for `batch/Job`.
+
+## Design Details
+
+### Workload API
+
+```go
+type PodSet struct {
+    // .......
+
+    // count is the number of pods for the spec.
+    // +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
+    Count int32 `json:"count"`
+
+    // minimumCount is the minimum number of pods for the spec acceptable
+    // in case of partial admission.
+    //
+    // If not provided, partial admission for the current PodSet is not
+    // enabled.
+    // +optional
+    MinimumCount *int32 `json:"minimumCount,omitempty"`
+}
+
+```
+
+### Scheduler / Flavorassignment
+
+In case the workload proposed for the current scheduling cycle, does not fit, with or without preemption, in the current available quota and any of its PodSets allow partial admission, try to find to find a lower counts combination that fits the available quota.
+
+The search should be optimized (binary search) and preserve the proportion of pods lost across the variable count PodSets.
+
+Starting with the PodSets:
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 4, MinCount: 2}, {Count: 20, MinCount: 10}}
+```
+
+And only being able to admit 19 pods, it should end up with 
+
+
+```go
+[]podSet { {Count: 1} , {Count: 3}, {Count: 15}}
+```
+
+With both pods that accept partial admission losing 50% of their range.
+
+
+The accepted number of pods in each PodSet are recorded in `workload.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[*].ResourceUsage.Count`
+
+### Jobframework
+
+```diff
+type GenericJob interface {
+    // ...
+
+	
+-    // RunWithNodeAffinity will inject the node affinity extracting from workload to job and unsuspend the job.
++    // RunWithPodSetsInfo will inject the node affinity and podsSet counts extracted from workload to the job and unsuspend the job.
+-    RunWithNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RunWithPodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+-    // RestoreNodeAffinity will restore the original node affinity of job.
++    // RestorePodSetsInfo will restore the original node affinity of job.
+-    RestoreNodeAffinity(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector)
++    RestorePodSetsInfo(nodeSelectors []PodSetNodeSelector, podSetCounts []int32)
+
+    // ...
+}
+
+```
+
+### batch/Job controller
+
+Besides adapting `RunWithPodSetsInfo` and `RestorePodSetsInfo` it should also:
+
+- rework `PodSets()` to populate `MinimumCount` if the job is marked to support partial admission.
+  * jobs supporting partial admission should have a dedicated annotation. eg. `kueue.x-k8s.io/job-min-parallelism`, indicating the minimum `parallelism` acceptable by the job in case of partial admission.
+  * jobs which need the `completions` count kept in sync with `parallelism` should indicate this in a second annotation `kueue.x-k8s.io/sync-completions`
+- rework `EquivalentToWorkload` to account for potential differences in `PodSets` spec `Parallelism`.
+
+### kubeflow/MPIJob controller
```

  There are no restrictions currently, and I don't think we want to impose any in JobSet, there is no justification to do so.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-05-23T16:57:08Z

- **keps/420-partial-admission/README.md:140** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-05-23T16:57:07Z

@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+# KEP-420: Allow partial admission of PodSets
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)

+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)

+  - [kubeflow/MPIJob controller](#kubeflowmpijob-controller)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+Add an optional way of allowing the partial admission of a workload if the full admission is not possible.
+
+## Motivation
+
+In practice, not all Workloads require the parallel execution of all the `count` of a `PodSet`, for such cases having a way to partially reserve the quota in order to prevent starvation.
+
+For example if a batch/Job has parallelism is x and there is only quota available for y < x then the job could still be admitted if it can work with a lower parallelism.
+
